<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" class="extiw" title="w:Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" class="extiw" title="w:Adolf Hitler">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Adolf_Hitler_Berghof-1936.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Adolf_Hitler_Berghof-1936.jpg/220px-Adolf_Hitler_Berghof-1936.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="318" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/ee/Adolf_Hitler_Berghof-1936.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="227" data-file-height="328"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Adolf_Hitler_Berghof-1936.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Adolf <b>Hitler</b> (German dictator)</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>The surname <i>Hitler</i> is a variation of <i>Hiedler</i>, a surname applied to those who resided near a <i class="Latn mention" lang="gsw"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hiedl&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hiedl (page does not exist)">Hiedl</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">subterranean river</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Udolph_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Udolph-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> Earlier theories<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> derived the surname from <i>Hüttler</i> (also spelled <i>Huettler</i>), either meaning "one who lives in a hut", from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/H%C3%BCtte#German" title="Hütte">Hütte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/h%C3%BCten#German" title="hüten">hüten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guard, look after</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Proper_noun">Proper noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">Hitler</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/surname" title="surname">surname</a> of <a href="/wiki/Austrian" title="Austrian">Austrian</a> <a href="/wiki/origin" title="origin">origin</a>.</li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" class="extiw" title="w:Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a>, dictator of <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> between 1933 and 1945.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1964</b>,  David Hugh Freeman,  <cite>A Philosophical Study of Religion</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?ei=LpDrTJ63JY6D4QavlbyZAQ&amp;ct=result&amp;id=gRgYAAAAIAAJ&amp;q=hitler#search_anchor">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The question makes no sense, unless the questioner is satisfied with such answers as: Death is evil, pain is evil, <b>Hitler</b> is evil.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1977</b>,  Peter Thomas Geach,  <cite>Providence and Evil</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=ohA8AAAAIAAJ&amp;lpg=PA40&amp;dq=hitler&amp;pg=PA41#v=onepage&amp;q=Hitler&amp;f=false">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Similarly, the description we give of God’s knowledge concerning <b>Hitler</b> has to be different after <b>Hitler</b>’s death; it is manifest that there has been a change on <b>Hitler</b>’s side, and that this, in view of the logic of omniscience, makes a difference to what we can truly say about God’s knowledge; ...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1994</b>,  Karen A. Rasler, William R. Thompson,  <cite>The great powers and global struggle, 1490-1990</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.co.uk/books?id=omAaTriUp0kC&amp;pg=PA188&amp;dq=%22if+hitler+had+never%22&amp;hl=en&amp;ei=o5PrTP_MEYuxhQf3lOFz&amp;sa=X&amp;oi=book_result&amp;ct=result&amp;resnum=7&amp;ved=0CEUQ6AEwBg#v=onepage&amp;q=%22if%20hitler%20had%20never%22&amp;f=false">[4]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Mueller is even less convincing in his suggestion that World War II might never have happened if <b>Hitler</b> had never been born.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Richard Dawkins,  <cite>The God Delusion</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=Ayt0bUwN5v4C&amp;lpg=PA133&amp;pg=PA133#v=onepage">[5]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">People do evil things (<b>Hitler</b>, Stalin, Saddam Hussein).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">Hitler</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Hitlers#English" title="Hitlers">Hitlers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unnecessarily <a href="/wiki/dictatorial" title="dictatorial">dictatorial</a> person.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  William Borman,  <cite>Gandhi and Non-Violence</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">How does he support his position against the <i>prima facie</i> case in favor of the strongly counterintuitive claim that non-violence would necessarily defeat a <b>Hitler</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
